Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Hwang Sun Jo
Reverend Sun Myung Moon, who at the age of 16 received a calling from Heaven for the salvation of humanity, has lived his life centered solely on the Heavenly Way. He described his life as follows:
"If Reverend Moon has any wealth, it is the suffering endured for public purposes rather than for myself. In social life, I have tried to suffer more than anyone else. In the providential position, I have tried to suffer more than anyone else. ... Reverend Moon has faced countless opposition and persecution from nations and the world. He was opposed in America, by Christianity, Judaism, and even communism. Never in history has the world united to attack one person with the intent to eliminate them. In that sense, Reverend Moon is a world champion.
However, despite being reviled, I have not been crushed or destroyed. I have emerged even stronger without the slightest tremor. ... Reverend Moon advocates for the liberation of humanity, the spirit world, hell, and even God." (Refer to Speech Collection Volume 105, pages 101-103)
Reverend Moon's life can be summed up in one word: 'suffering.' This suffering is not for himself but for God and humanity. From this, we understand who he is. Reverend Moon is the Second Coming and Savior that Christianity has hoped for over 2000 years, and he has come as the True Parent of humanity. Already, disciples in 185 countries around the world are following Reverend Moon, realizing the ideal of the True Family to walk the path of True Children with this confession of faith.
Reverend Moon's identity is verified through his words and life. He possesses a truth that does not exist in the world. The issues of God and humanity, history, and the world are clarified in his words. The promise of new words prophesied in the Bible is fulfilled in him, setting us free. These words contain 'life.' More importantly, Reverend Moon's words are merely an 'interpretation of his own life.' In other words, he himself is the truth. The Word became flesh, that is, incarnated. Therefore, life itself is the truth, and it approaches us through the framework of 'words.'
I am confident that readers will understand Reverend Moon's greatness through his words. Although the level of Reverend Moon's words is too high and deep to fully comprehend, they fundamentally have three characteristics.
First, Reverend Moon revealed God through his words and life. He liberated God from silence and suffering. Because humans have the lineage of evil, they cannot be called children, causing God's suffering. Reverend Moon made the sorrowful God, who was tragically alienated by human sin, 'speak.' He made God, who was silent in the confines of church authority, doctrine, and ornate buildings, 'speak,' and made God, who could not come as a parent, 'become a parent,' making Reverend Moon 'the complete revelation of God.'
Secondly, Reverend Moon liberated humanity from ignorance and confusion. Although we humans have the ability to think and make value judgments, we cannot deny the tragic reality of not fully understanding our own existence. Moreover, although humans are not independent beings and are interdependent with others, they have not clarified this relationship. The reason is that they lost God's words. Reverend Moon provides the ultimate answer to this. Furthermore, through a life that upholds the Heavenly Way, he shows a concrete path as an example. Therefore, his words are living words full of life.
Thirdly, Reverend Moon liberated the world of all things. Every object created by God is an individual truth body with inherent value. Although its value should be fully realized under the original dominion of a true human, it has not been, causing all things to groan. Reverend Moon clarified the original value of the world of all things through his words and opened the way for the liberation of all things by restoring humans to their original state.
Reverend Moon and his wife, who came as the eternal True Parents of humanity, continue to speak tirelessly around the world today, setting an example of living with the heart of a parent and the body of a servant, teaching to 'live for the sake of others,' and working hard to inherit true love, true life, and true lineage.
Additionally, through the words of life, noble life, and achievements, Reverend Moon has finally restored God's sovereignty as we enter the new millennium, establishing himself as the King of Blessed Families on this earth. He has created the Peace UN, binding the world into one realm of heart, aiming for the Kingdom of Peace, Cheon Il Guk, the Fourth Israel, the Kingdom of Peace.
I hope that the readers who encounter these words will become the owners of Cheon Il Guk and the main actors in building the Kingdom of Peace. *

1)
Teach about God and the Spirit World
(Reports from Leaders on the Preparation for the 'Cheonji Parents' Settlement Rally')
The most important issue for humans is to know God and the spirit world. 
We will do this for 20 days from now. It would be good to have more locations if possible. We must operate electronic billboards and monitors, making it a turning point. We cannot ignore the spirit world. We must know God and the spirit world. That is the most important issue for humans.
Philosophy and religion currently have uncertain perspectives, whether Confucianism, Buddhism, Islam, Christianity, or even communism, they cannot deny the testimony of 120 people. We must organize this separately into books, whether it is Buddhism or Confucianism. This will give religious people a clear perspective on what we have said. Has anyone taught about the spirit world in detail until now? That is the most important thing. (Report continues)
June 1, 2002 (Saturday) night, Hannam International Training Center.
* This speech was given at the dining table, and the title was added by the editor.
10   Teach about God and the Spirit World
We need a new revolution in the religious world.
Call Yang Chang-sik. (Phone call begins) Who is this? Are you sick? Why do you sound so weak? How is the atmosphere in America while the World Cup is happening here? Is there no interest in America? "America is the least interested place in the world right now. (President Kwak Jeong-hwan)" Really?
How is the blessing of young people by pastors going? The sons and daughters of pastors, those in Ivy League schools, we can encourage them to participate in university activities.... The Unification Church has a good chance this time. We must tie the pastors together. By doing so, we can bring all the youth to church and make it possible for them to gather.
We must stimulate the pastors in this way, so that students come to church, and those who graduate from university connect with university students, and university students connect with their alma mater's middle and high schools. We must organize the nation as a system centered on school connections.
In the provinces, they must visit schools. Aren't there pastors in schools? They must visit the school chaplains. They must establish connections and give lectures at schools. There are students who participated in the 'Lasting Love Conference,' right? If they are students from socialist countries, we must plan to involve them in blessing those studying in America. Do you understand what I mean?
And what is the public opinion after the Washington Times anniversary banquet meeting? We must remove the church crosses. Do you understand? We must start this movement for Christianity to survive. We must shock them by saying, 'Oh, our faith was a lie. We were deceived.' They must think anew and plant new roots to develop into a new dimension.
This is an important issue. It is not something that can end as a passing rumor. The root and essence of the spirit world are changing. What is the doctrine of the cross? It is the doctrine of resurrection. It is inevitable. Even the Bible is structured that way.
And by removing the cross, the Jews must repent for their mistakes. The Jews themselves, why have they been massacred for 2,000 years, why were 6 million killed by Hitler, they have no way to interpret it even in their dreams. 'Ah, it was because of the sin of killing Jesus, who was to become the True Parent.' They must be able to accept Jesus as the Messiah for the first Israel to be resurrected. Since they did not have the rebirth ceremony, they must go through the rebirth, resurrection, and eternal life ceremonies again.
There was no way to connect with Jesus until now, was there? There are only 2.8% Christians in the Jewish nation now, right? So they were punished. If the Jews continue as they did in the past, they must be expelled. Do you understand?
We must make the pastors voluntarily pray and remove the crosses. Tell them about our seminary. Say that Heaven struck with lightning and removed the crosses. That awakened them.
What I did this time was to create a new revolution in the religious world, and by admitting that they have believed wrongly until now, the opposition from the right and communists will completely overturn. The impact is significant. While doing this, what it means is that Jesus died because he could not marry. Isn't that so? Therefore, the blessing is automatically opened, to the clergy. We must instill such thoughts in the Roman Catholic Church and the heads of the American denominations to play the game of removing the cross. Do you understand?
12   Teach about God and the Spirit World
Follow the path of the Second Coming True Parents.
Did you hear that I am holding a rally here on the 21st? From the 21st, we must teach the entire United States about the reality of the spirit world. Do you understand? Christianity, Confucianism, Buddhism, Hinduism, Islam, even communism, then the university federation, then the media, then the U.S. President, the Japanese Emperor, and the Korean King, focusing on the ancestors who went to the spirit world from these three countries, the kings of the past, they must gather and be educated on the path they must take.... Isn't that so? They must follow the path of the Second Coming and True Parents. That is the providential view.
Therefore, the mission of religion is to end once they receive the blessing. In the end, it is to organize families transcending ethnicity, centering on their nation, to create one world. This family organization is the purpose of religion. Therefore, the religious sphere will not enter the heavenly kingdom on earth and in heaven. Cheon Il Guk is not something any religion does. It is God's nation and the people of heaven. Once they become the people of heaven, born in the homeland and native land of heaven, without Satan, they must know such things.
How many national messiahs are there? Should we call all the national messiahs here for the Day of All Things, or should they direct themselves? Should we let them come and go?
Didn't we connect our video center worldwide through satellite before? So, centering on the 21st, we must inform the entire world about the reality of the spirit world, focusing on Korea, Japan, and the United States. Christianity, Buddhism, Confucianism, Islam, then communism, then the university federation, the media, their ancestors! The ancestors must educate the representatives of each country and announce, 'Our people, listen!' Do you understand?
First, centering on Korea, Japan, and the United States, the ancestors in the spirit world must say that they must believe in True Parents, then follow the coming Second Coming. We must establish this firmly. So, after creating a booklet, we must distribute it and give lectures as it is. After starting the lecture on that day, we must connect directly with Reverend Moon through satellite and deliver the message, then announce it as the declaration of True Parents.
We must mobilize as many people as possible in each country. We must mobilize the peace ambassadors and hold rallies to inform the world. Otherwise, the spirit world cannot cooperate. Do you understand? The spirit world is taking a united front through a unified main direction, but there is no way to connect this united front system vertically.
If the earth is the Abel-type entity, the Cain-type entity must serve the Abel-type entity. This system must be in place. Since the work is happening centered on blessed families, the global blessed families have the responsibility to inform the world.
True Parents, with the permission of God through the Unification Church leaders in the spirit world, have taught the secrets of heaven and earth, and this is the benefit received from True Parents. They express gratitude for the education they received and wish to inform all people of the world, transcending religion, nation, and NGO.
This was sent to connect with the blessed families of the Unification Church, centering on Reverend Moon, to become a united entity that allows the spirit world to operate. Once this is announced, the minions of Lucifer who have opposed God's will until now must cooperate if they do not want to pack up and leave. They must cooperate. Do you understand?
The spirits who have opposed God's will until now must turn around and cooperate. To completely indemnify and liberate, even the spirits who worked in Satan's world must be liberated in the spirit world and are now in training centers. Therefore, even those minions must cooperate. Cain and Abel must unite. The Cain family and the Abel family must unite for complete judgment to occur. Do you understand? They are clinging to the remaining connections between the spirit world and the physical world, not wanting to let go. So, it must be announced on earth. Do you understand?
Then, from Jesus to Buddha, Confucius, Mohammed, communist leaders, then the royal families of those countries, then the media, then the education federation! Once all of this is done, all the leaders who have influenced the world will be included. Since they all conclude that they must follow True Parents, there is no one on earth who can oppose. It can be swept clean. Do you understand?
Prepare and do so, consulting with Hwang Sun Jo here. I cannot always call you, can I? (Report from President Yang Chang-sik)
Life must be unified with the standard of the spirit world.
Do you understand? National messiahs must receive through satellite and hold rallies to clearly teach the people about God and the 'reality of the spirit world.' We must create a unified standard for the world spirits to cooperate with the representatives of each country. Do you understand?
All living and eating must be unified with the standard of the spirit world. Therefore, the world must completely offer everything. The ownership of nations, the ownership of all humans, must be returned to God, and True Parents must collectively return it and then distribute it. What was returned to Satan due to the fall of evil parents must be restored and returned, becoming the property of God, and then reallocated according to the instructions of True Parents to become the original nation. Teach this clearly.
Now, contact Mr. Hwang and do it together. (End of phone call)
Not all national messiahs need to come. Just bring one representative from each of the six continents. Ah, what a good time the world is in! This time, we must thoroughly shake up Japan.... (Subsequent report from President Hwang Sun Jo on the satellite broadcast of the event) *

We Were Born for Others

"...We have come to know the two beings, God as the subject and humans as the object. And we have come to know that these two must inevitably become one. But even if God Himself thinks about where to place the origin of true love, true happiness, true peace, true ideals, and true freedom, it cannot help but be a problem."

Why must we live for others? Why must we live for others? Even God's perfection is achieved through living for others. Love, everything, cannot manifest in a place where there is no living for others. If everything ends with living for today, tomorrow we look for something greater, but today's things cannot fill tomorrow's ideals. So, when the environment changes, in a place where you can love and digest it and live for it, infinite development continues.

Therefore, no matter how much love, life, and ideals God has, these are not achieved by Himself. They are achieved through the object. Since the object is the one that can achieve these, the object is the one that achieves them, so He finds all ideals in living for the object. Do you understand what I'm saying? "Yes."

God cannot achieve completion by Himself. Completion is achieved through the object. Love and everything else, even the ideal realm of the universe, cannot be achieved by having it alone. It is achieved through the object.

So, nothing in the world was born for itself. No woman was born for herself. Do you understand? "Yes." A woman's ideal, a woman's love, a woman's life itself cannot be completed without a man. For a man, the core of the highest ideal truth is a woman, and for a woman, the core that completes all ideal conditions is a man.

Since such precious things are not achieved by oneself but by the object, the greater happiness and the greater world are sought in living for the object. Therefore, the ideal world and utopia can exist there. You must understand this. Do you understand? "Yes."

There is no way to deny the logic that we were born for others. When you look at your eyes, were they born to see themselves? Were they born for themselves? They were born for the object. When you have a nose, was it born for itself? "No." It was born to smell! Whose smell? Your own smell? (Laughter) For the object!

The same goes for speaking. Why do you have a mouth? To speak! Do you speak looking at your own mouth, looking at your own face? For the object! Why do you have ears? Were they born to speak, or to listen? For the object! Why do hands move? They don't move for themselves, but to expand the relationship with the object!

So, for a person to complete themselves, they must be in a position where they can live more for others, but the body and mind of a person fight. Why do they fight? This is a big problem. Isn't it? Love was not created for oneself 
『……If humans had not originally fallen, they would have accepted God's tradition of living for others and formed this world into a world of peace, a heaven on earth. Despite this, searching for a path centered on oneself from self-awareness and exploration is what the fall is.』 
What is the most precious thing for men and women? It's their life organ. The life organ is the reproductive organ. A woman's reproductive organ was not created for herself. It's for a man. Do you understand, you men? "Yes." Why are you lying down like that? Are you hungry? Where did my watch go? What time is it? "It's nine o'clock." Where is the watch? It's covered! 

The champion who reads Hoon Dok Hae the most diligently is the teacher 

What time is it? "It's nine o'clock." It's nine o'clock, nine o'clock. (Laughter) That's how you think. "The clock went fast." Tomorrow morning, don't do that. Then tomorrow, when it's ten o'clock, think, "It's ten o'clock because I rested for a few hours." 

Don't think like a merchant who made a loss. If you have invested an hour more than others in the purpose, the business is good or bad? It's good. It is definitely accumulated in the heavenly kingdom. How many thousands, tens of thousands, hundreds of thousands of hours of Hoon Dok Hae will you have? The champion who reads Hoon Dok Hae the most diligently is the teacher, is it you? Hwang Seon-jo, right? "It's the Parents." Kim Hyo-yul, right? Yoo Jeong-ok, right? 

It has to be fun, fun. Interest and fun! Is fun better, or is interest better? Fun is when you feel it in a relative relationship, and interest is when there is no relative relationship. If you have an interest in this meeting, you sit here, but what relationship is there? Liking it alone is interest. That's different. Now! 

"...Until now, the Father had no country. There were no people. There was no territory. Now, from now on, God's sons and daughters who can form a people for the Father will emerge, and the Father will combine these sons and daughters to create families, combine families to create a nation, move a nation to create a global foundation internally." 

Have you blessed them, blessed them? You blessed a lot in the 1980s, right? Did you do all 180 families? Even if it's 190 families or 2,000 families, it's fine. You have to manage it. When Christmas comes, have you ever sent a gift wrapped in tissue paper because you have no money? 

You are a mother and father. You must become a mother and father. If you just give birth, what is that? It's a reckless mother and father. You are a mother and father who can be cursed by your children. In the spirit world, it becomes like that. Now, the authority to register in the heavenly kingdom has been given. If you offer devotion for more than three years, you must give them a card, having blessed them. 

What are the children of faith? Are the children of faith precious, or are your own children, who are not blessed, precious? "The children of faith are precious." The children of faith are precious. The world doesn't know, so... Now! (End of reading the speech for the 2nd Day of All Things) 

Yoon Jeong-ro, bring the manuscript, the manuscript. Read it again. Will Yoon Jeong-ro read it? You rest a little. This is the content to be talked about on the 12th at the Little Angels. Listen. (Director Yoon Jeong-ro reads the speech for the Sun Moon Peace Cup Soccer Tournament Inauguration Ceremony on June 12) 

Era of Liberation of the Victory of the Autonomous Nation and the Era of Original One Unification 

Shall we stop? "Yes, it's finished. (Yoon Jeong-ro)" It will be done on the 12th, and on the 14th, the mother will do it, but I also have to talk. Without a manuscript, I plan to do a lot of Hoon Dok Hae, spiritual world messages. Then it must end with the meeting on the 21st. Therefore, the spiritual world must be fully mobilized and grafted to the earth. 

So, you must now make your blessed family, following your own clan, the owner of a nation along with the ancestor Dangun of Korea. There is no nation belonging to God. You must graft it to liberate all nations, all the nations that have joined the UN. Therefore, you must register in the world countries. Your current registration is to register in a nation. 

So, to register in Cheon Il Guk, you must meet the era of liberation of the autonomous nation and establish the victory of the autonomous nation to be liberated. What is the victory of the autonomous nation? It is to escape the satanic world without falling. By escaping, you meet the era of liberation. Therefore, it is the era of liberation of the victory of the autonomous nation. Since the era of liberation has formed the shape of the creation ideal, it is Original One. You must graft it to the original root. It cannot be done as it is because of the fall. 

Centering on the creation ideal of the Garden of Eden, you must create a single nation, a single cultural world of the Adam family, Adam clan, and Adam nation. But because a complex and diverse mixed nation was created, you must match it to a single nation, an Original One single nation. You must match it to a single unified world, an Original One unified world. There is a large gear, and to match it, you must cut the gear and match it here, otherwise, the rotating universe will break down. 

So, what is the Original One? It is the era of unification. You must unify. Only then is it complete liberation. God, from the heavenly world to the earthly world, becomes one family with the blessed people of the heavenly world, the True Parents' family, and the True Parents' bloodline, and through the realization of the heavenly world, the earthly world, and the heavenly world, the heavenly kingdom is achieved. 

What is Cheon Il Guk? 'Cheon' (heaven) is the combination of two (二) people (人). It is a nation where heaven is united, where more than two people are united, which is Cheon Il Guk. All things are in pairs. From the insect world to animals, they are in pairs, and even minerals are in pairs. They must become one. By giving and receiving, a center is created. When it moves like this, a core is inevitably created. A core is created. 

That core is vertical, and there is a family core. In the family, if it is a man, the man's body and mind must become one to be the individual core. They are not one, right? God cannot reside in the center. They must become one. It must become horizontal and rotate 360 degrees, but it cannot rotate like this. Because it becomes horizontal, it is invisible. 

From that position, it rotates, and that individual center must connect with the family center, the clan, the nation, the world... It must establish a relationship with the 8 stages of the universe. The era of liberation of the victory of the autonomous nation, then, after liberation, it is not about playing as you please. Centering on the cosmic parents, you must become the center of eternal unchanging individual perfection, family perfection, clan, nation, world... 8 stages of perfection. Only then can you register in the heavenly kingdom. The world also has individual restoration, family restoration, clan restoration, nation restoration, world restoration, cosmic restoration, even God, 8 stages. 

Since the Declaration of the Eight Great Textbooks has been made, you must declare it all. It has been declared. This time, on the 21st, it is the era of the settlement of the Cosmic Parents. Settlement and establishment are different. It must be settled so that everything can live together. Establishment means starting. Since it is established, it must be settled. I said it is the era of settlement, not the era of establishment. It must be written as the era of settlement. You read it all, right? "Yes." 

Until the 12th, it will be done, and on the 14th, what will be done will be done in the morning. I was going to do it all today, but a lot of time has passed. Do you understand? "Yes." Then, let's pray... (Director Yoon Jeong-ro prays) (Bows) 

Let's create a storm with spiritual messages 

(Front part not recorded) Somehow, a great transformation is happening in America. They must repent, the pastors related to the church must pray to God and remove the cross and erect the tower of resurrection. Heaven is at a loss. 

So, don't they oppose Reverend Moon? "Father, there is no opposition at all now. (Yang Chang-shik)" They are all saying to remove the cross... "It needs some explanation, but surprisingly, the pastors' reactions are sincere." Reaction? They must think there is no other way. Why must there be a second coming? The very idea of completing salvation through the second coming is contradictory. You must set the Ivy League students of America on fire. 

"Father, I will briefly report on Thailand and the Philippines. (Kim Byung-woo)" Thailand, Thailand. "There wasn't enough time... As you instructed last time, we made CDs with the messages from communist leaders and Christian leaders. Helen Smith, who toured with Mother, has a very good voice. It was done at our studio in Manhattan, and it sounds very good. (Yang Chang-shik)" The communists... During the election, you must continue in every neighborhood, whether they like it or not. It's a big fuss, all of them. 

"At the UN headquarters conference in Bangkok, we held a seminar with members of the Professors Academy and VIPs who helped us, including senators and congressmen, with 200 people at the UN conference hall. It was an all-day event, and this person, who protected us, is a former chairman of the Joint Chiefs of Staff and has been involved with our 'World Summit Council.' This person is very grateful. He is now the current chairman of the Central Election Management Committee and has been handling our work. We are now in the 12th year of legal battles and are preparing for a total counterattack. So, at this gathering of senators and congressmen, we introduced a part of our principle and, on the occasion of the UN Family Day, introduced our principle. It was all reported on TV." 

From now on, you must hold onto the congressmen and strip them of their shells. Make them all receive training and become peace ambassadors... "It's the UN headquarters conference, but we rented the main conference hall."
Holding such a gathering at our Unification Church is an event in Thailand. (Chairman Kim Byung-woo shows a photo album and reports on the church construction in Thailand and the Philippines.)

"...This time, the university that awarded my wife a Ph.D. in English is expressing interest in inviting Hyun Jin Nim, and this news is spreading among universities, with university presidents showing interest in inviting Hyun Jin Nim." Really? "...There is a university with about 24,000 students. They also want to invite us, so currently, three universities are expressing interest in inviting Hyun Jin Nim." That would be great!

"...There is a very expensive Norwegian-style fish cage, and then there is a cheaper fish cage made in the Philippines. Looking at the fish, there are 30,000 to 40,000 fish growing inside the cage. They say that if you raise these fish for just two months, they can be sold on the market. We were very impressed by this." Isn't that something we were planning to do? "So the government here only charges a tax for renting the location. The tax is about $500 a year, and they rent out the location, and if we just make the cages, the government plans to distribute them." 

Gwak Jung-hwan! "Yes." Did you budget everything at 1,000 something? Was it 1.3 million dollars? "At that time..." Palau! "Not Palau, here..." Didn't we plan to do that in Palau too? "Not Palau, but here, the Speaker of the Indonesian Parliament mentioned a $12 million unit, a $7 million unit, and a $4 million unit. That's what was said at the time, right?" We're doing all of that.

"Yes, so a sample site has been established. It doesn't cost much, and seeing it in operation, we found it quite promising. We are placing fish cages in various locations and waiting for investment." Aren't we doing that in Jeju Island now? "Yes, it's a very good resort area. This is a scene from seminars held in each region, leadership seminars." Park Gu-bae is planning to do it on a large scale.

"So, if Chairman Gwak comes and sees it, he will be able to make significant plans for the future. This is the first time something like this has come out. The Philippine government also says that fish are drying up, and because the fishing methods are primitive, they can't accommodate the fish." It's something that can be left over. "So they realized the need for aquaculture, and the government is making cages, and if there is private investment, they will rent out locations and just make the cages to raise fish. That's the current discussion." The cages can be easily assembled. We can make them with fiber like the ones used for making boats.

This person, who was a journalist helping us, is now going to Poland as an ambassador. So if you get Father's signature... This is the scene where he takes the oath in front of the President. He wanted to get a signature from Father. This is the scene where he receives the appointment letter from the President. He is like family to us. He received a blessing. He went out as the ambassador to Poland. Is the ambassador to Poland important? "It's not important, but because he made a significant contribution to us..." You know if it's important to you, coming late at night and asking the teacher for a signature? You have the mindset of a thief. June? "The 10th." The 10th! What's his name? "Andrew, Andrew Rosario." Andrew Rosario!

"Now, if Father acknowledges this, it will become a real doctorate. Park Jung-hae!" Park Jung-hae! "This is a report of all the activities that have been done so far." Park Jung-hae? "Yes." Is there nothing else now? "Yes, that's it." (Laughter) Signing for doctorates and such will be busy in the future. You should carve a stamp for signing and hang it where you live, and stamp it one by one, it's so noisy.

Well, since everyone worked hard, it's all necessary. The history of the Unification Church being chased out and almost collapsing is quite harsh, isn't it? This time, no one said they didn't trust the Unification Church, at least not to me.

Song Young-seok, Argentina is now in a mess, and there's nothing left to salvage, what should we do? "It will be fine after a while. Once we overcome the indemnity, it will be sorted out." Who is the current president? "Juan..." The former president is saying he will run again, right? "Yes, he can't run for a third term next year, so he's being set aside, but he's coming out this time, but his image is not good..." If he had followed my words, it wouldn't be like this. "So he can't come out." But they say he's coming out? They say he's coming out.

What time is it now? "It's 11:20." Eleven o'clock? (Bow) What time? What time is the flight tomorrow? "Yes, it's at seven o'clock." Then will Gwak Jung-hwan conduct the Hoon Dok Hae tomorrow? "We'll continue with the official program as scheduled, and later, we'll arrange to report separately to receive Father's supervision, and the ceremony will proceed according to the official schedule."*
